\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{signal}{signal}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct signal signal}

Signals map CAN data to physical signals and provide units, conversion factors and data types. The same as used in CANdb++. \Hypertarget{_c_a_n1db_8h_a8f216c36633c7ff47dfb4231aaa6d2a4}\label{_c_a_n1db_8h_a8f216c36633c7ff47dfb4231aaa6d2a4} 
\index{CAN1db.h@{CAN1db.h}!signal\_positioned@{signal\_positioned}}
\index{signal\_positioned@{signal\_positioned}!CAN1db.h@{CAN1db.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{signal\_positioned}{signal\_positioned}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct signal\+\_\+positioned signal\+\_\+positioned}

Each message contains a struct of type \doxylink{structsignal__positioned}{signal\+\_\+positioned} to indicate the signal\textquotesingle{}s position in the can frame and to allow access of the signals properties using a pointer.
